function onShadowboxClose (e) {
	Shadowbox.fortunaOnClose();

    var _onCloseCallback = $('#page-variables').attr('data-shadowboxonclose')
    // zavolani callback metody, je-li nastavena v page-variables

function _evaluateCommand ( command, e ) {
    commands[command]
        ? commands[command](e)
        : _runCallbackFromString( command, e)
}

function _runCallbackFromString( methodName, e ) {
    var _fn = FORTUNA.UTILS.getFnFromString(methodName, FORTUNA.UI)

    _fn && _fn(e)
}

    window.location.reload();
